DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:stable-slim
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      cmake \
      git \
      libsystemd-dev \
      pkg-config \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      python3-venv \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN python3 -c "import sys; print(sys.path)" && \
      python3 -m ensurepip --upgrade && \
      python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel || \
      (echo "Python environment setup failed" && python3 -m pip debug && exit 1)
  COPY . .
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir --verbose -r requirements.txt || \
      (echo "Failed to install Python packages" && \
       cat /home/cc/EnvGym/requirements.txt && \
       python3 -m pip debug && exit 1)
  RUN mkdir -p build && \
      cd build && \
      cmake .. || (echo "CMake configuration failed" && exit 1) && \
      make || (echo "Build failed" && exit 1) && \
      make install || (echo "Installation failed" && exit 1)
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  COPY . .
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir --verbose -r requirements.txt --retries 5 --timeout 60
  RUN mkdir -p build && \
      cd build && \
      cmake .. && \
      make && \
      make install
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM debian:stable-slim
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      cmake \
      git \
      libsystemd-dev \
      pkg-config \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      python3-venv \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN python3 -c "import urllib.request; urllib.request.urlopen('https://pypi.org')" || (echo "Network connectivity check failed" && exit 1)
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip --no-cache-dir --default-timeout=100 --retries 5 --no-warn-script-location || \
      python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip --no-cache-dir --default-timeout=100 --no-warn-script-location
  RUN python3 -m pip install --upgrade setuptools wheel --no-cache-dir --default-timeout=100 --retries 5 --no-warn-script-location || \
      python3 -m pip install --upgrade setuptools wheel --no-cache-dir --default-timeout=100 --no-warn-script-location
  COPY . .
  RUN python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir --verbose -r requirements.txt --default-timeout=100 --retries 5 --no-warn-script-location || \
      python3 -m pip install --no-cache-dir --verbose -r requirements.txt --default-timeout=100 --no-warn-script-location
  RUN mkdir -p build && \
      cd build && \
      cmake .. && \
      make && \
      make install
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym

      python3 -m pip install --upgrade setuptools wheel --no-cache-dir --default-timeout=100 --verbose

      cmake .. && \
      make && \
      make install || \
      (echo "Build failed" && exit 1)
